<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Römer</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рябой.html>рябо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rjabój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)рябе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:рябь.html>рябе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pitted, pocked, pockmarked</li>
<li>speckled</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A special short form is found in the name of the fairy-tale character <i class="None mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курочка.html>ку́рочка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рябой.html>ря́ба</a></b></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ryaba the Hen</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Speckled Hen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This form is an old short attributive feminine singular.</li></ul>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рябина.html>ряби́на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rjabína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рявкать.html>ря́вкать</a> (24305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рявкать.html>ря́вкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rjávkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рявкнуть.html>ря́вкнуть</a></b>)

<p><b>ря́в<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***ряд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a> (182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">рѧдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rędŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rędъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">рѧдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rędŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (translating <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τάξις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">táxis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">διαδοχή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">diadokhḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ре̑д</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">rȇd</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">řád</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">rád</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rjad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́да</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряда́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>рядо́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* After the numbers 2, 3, and 4, the stress falls on the last syllable: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">62 <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряда́</a></span>.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>row, line, tier
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:передний.html>пере́днем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряду́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sidétʹ v perédnem <b>rjadú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit in the front <b>row</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>file, rank</li>
<li>series
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степенной.html>степе́нного</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">predél stepénnovo <b>rjáda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the limit of a power <b>series</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:последовать.html>после́довал</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подозрительный.html>подозри́тельных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происшествие.html>происше́ствий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poslédoval <b>rjad</b> podozrítelʹnyx proisšéstvij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there followed a <b>series</b> of suspicious incidents</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>a number of, several
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́де</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чаев</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>rjáde</b> slúčajev</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in <b>several</b> cases</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> degree of backness or frontness
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:передний.html>пере́днего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́да</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glásnyje <b>perédnevo rjáda</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>front</b> vowels</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядить.html>ряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ordain <i>(that)</i>, to lay down the law</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contract</li></ol>

<p><b>ря<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>

<p><b>ря<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>

Зализняка — 4b.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ряд-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядовой.html>рядово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rjadovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> row, line
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рядовой.html>рядовы́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:культура.html>культу́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rjadovýje</b> kulʹtúry</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>row</b> crops</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ordinary, common, average, routine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rank and file
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рядовой.html>рядово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:состав.html>соста́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rjadovój</b> sostáv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>rank and file</b> membership</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***с.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> (10)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ(n)</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">s</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́м</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>s</b> (moím) brátom</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>with</b> (my) brother</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мое́й</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестро́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>s</b> (mojéj) sestrój</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>with</b> (my) sister</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>so</b> vsémi</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>with</b> everybody</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>so</b> mnoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>with</b> me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>s</b> tobój</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>with</b> you</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>from, off, from off, from below <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with abstract nouns; nouns entailing a flat, open area; and special exceptions; + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поле.html>по́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>s</b> pólja</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>from</b> the field</span></div></dd>

<li>because of, since <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">expressing a cause of motivation; + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>s</b> ispúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>due to</b> being frightened</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>for, about <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating indefinite time or number</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>from <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating a duration of time; + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:главный.html>гла́вного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здание.html>зда́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проводиться.html>проводи́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятый.html>пя́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:январь.html>января́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седьмой.html>седьмо́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:февраль.html>февраля́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Remónt glávnovo zdánija búdet provodítʹsja <b>s</b> dvádcatʹ pjátovo janvarjá po sedʹmóje fevraljá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The renovation of the main building will be conducted <b>from</b> January 25th to February 7th.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in certain time expressions; + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>When indicating a duration of time, the normal expression is either <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> or <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A noun phrase with the preposition <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and an abstract noun declined with the instrumental case can show adverb-like qualities. The most notable ones are below:
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́нием</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s vnimánijem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>трудо́м</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s trudóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрип.html>скри́пом</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">so skrípom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствием</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s udovólʹstvijem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sovsém</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul></li></ul>

<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">санти-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">santi-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>., <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> твор. п. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чаев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:избежание.html>избежа́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стечение.html>стече́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:согласный.html>согла́сных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стык.html>сты́ке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a></i>; <i><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-с-</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бля</a> (7699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">саблѩ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sablję</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sabľa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бля</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sáblja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бель</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">са́бельный</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">са́белька</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>saber, cutlass</li>
<li>cavalryman <i>(used as a unit of count, see also <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штык</a>)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эскадрон.html>эскадро́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двести.html>две́сти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сабля.html>са́бель</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">eskadrón v dvésti <b>sábelʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a squadron of two hundred cavalrymen</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***саботаж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:саботаж.html>сабота́ж</a> (19845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sabotage</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саботаж.html>сабота́ж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sabotáž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саботаж.html>сабота́жа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саботаж.html>сабота́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саботаж.html>сабота́жей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dereliction (non-execution, very slow or careless execution, of one's duties)</li>
<li>sabotage (deliberate action of subversion, obstruction, disruption, destruction)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:саботажник.html>сабота́жник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sabotážnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">саботи́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sabotírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
